Shareholders should refer to the offer restrictions included in the section titled &#8220;Important information&#8221; at the end of this announcement and in the offer document, which has been published on the Offer website (www.smokefree-offer.com). Shareholders in the United States should also refer to the section entitled &#8220;Special notice to shareholders in the United States&#8221; at the end of this announcement.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:right"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">Press release </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">November 10, 2022</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:14pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">PMHH acquires shares in Swedish Match outside the offer and becomes the owner of nearly 86% of the shares</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">On May 11, 2022, Philip Morris Holland Holdings B.V.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.8pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%;position:relative;top:-4.2pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%"> (&#8220;PMHH</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">&#8221;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">), an affiliate of Philip Morris International Inc. (&#8220;PMI</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">&#8221;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">), announced a recommended public offer to the shareholders of Swedish Match AB (&#8220;Swedish Match</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">&#8221;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">) to tender all shares in Swedish Match</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.8pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%;position:relative;top:-4.2pt;vertical-align:baseline">2</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%"> to PMHH (the</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#160;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">&#8220;Offer</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">&#8221;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">). On November 7, 2022, PMHH declared the Offer unconditional and announced that it would complete the Offer and acquire all shares in Swedish Match that have been tendered in the Offer. In addition, PMHH extended the acceptance period until November 25, 2022 and informed the Swedish Match shareholders that the price in the Offer for shares tendered during the further extended acceptance period will be reduced to SEK 115.07 in cash per share due to the resolved dividend payment by Swedish Match of SEK 0.93 per share for shareholders of record as of November 14, 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">The shares tendered in the Offer at the end of the acceptance period (which expired on November 4, 2022) amounted to in aggregate 1,255,989,816 shares in Swedish Match</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">3</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">, corresponding to approximately 82.59 percent</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">4</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%"> of the share capital and the voting rights in Swedish Match. Settlement for shares tendered in the Offer up to and including November 4, 2022, is expected to be initiated around November 11, 2022.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#333333;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">As set forth in the offer document regarding the Offer made public on June 28, 2022 (the &#8220;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#333333;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">Offer Document</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#333333;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#8221;),</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%"> PMHH and its affiliates may, to the extent permissible under applicable law or regulations, acquire, or take measures to acquire, shares in Swedish Match in other ways than through the Offer. Information about such acquisitions of shares, or measures to acquire shares, must be disclosed in accordance with applicable laws and regulations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt;text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt;text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div shares).</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;text-align:justify"><font Accordingly, the total number of shares in Swedish Match acquired by PMHH, including the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">shares tendered in the Offer at the end of the acceptance period on November 4, 2022, amounts to 1,305,889,764 shares, corresponding to approximately 85.87 percent</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">5</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%"> of the share capital and the voting rights in Swedish Match. We will be working together to create value as we accelerate towards our shared vision of a smoke-free future.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">PMHH will continue to strive towards an ownership in Swedish Match of more than 90 percent</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">5</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%"> of the total number of shares in Swedish Match and thereafter initiate compulsory redemption of the remaining shares in Swedish Match under the Swedish Companies Act (Sw. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">aktiebolagslagen</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%"> (2005&#58;551)), as well as promote a delisting of Swedish Match&#8217;s shares from Nasdaq Stockholm. For further information on the implications of PMHH&#8217;s ownership of less than 90 percent of the total number of registered shares in Swedish Match, PMHH refers shareholders of Swedish Match to the description thereof included in the section of the Offer Document entitled &#8220;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">Important notice to shareholders in the United States of America</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">&#8221;.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6.75pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">As previously announced, PMHH has extended the acceptance period until November 25, 2022 at 17.00 (CET) to provide the remaining shareholders of Swedish Match who have not tendered their shares time to accept the Offer. Due to the resolved dividend payment by Swedish Match of SEK 0.93 per share with record date for the payment on November 14, 2022, and expected date for payment through Euroclear Sweden on November 17, 2022, the price in the Offer for shares tendered during the further extended acceptance period will, in accordance with the terms and conditions of the Offer</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">6</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">, be reduced accordingly to SEK 115.07 in cash per share. For further information regarding Swedish Match&#8217;s resolution on dividends at the annual general meeting 2022, please refer to Swedish Match&#8217;s website,&#160;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%;text-decoration:underline">www.swedishmatch.com</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">. 2022, the SEK 0.93 dividend payment will not be received by PMHH, but by the shareholder registered as of the record date on November 14, 2022.</font></div><div
